Each window corresponds to a single trading day's session\n * (e.g., NYSE 09:30-16:00 ET, LSE 08:00-16:30 GMT).\n *\n * <p>Events are assigned to the session window for the trading day that their timestamp falls in.\n * If an event's timestamp is before the session open on a given day, it is grouped with that day's\n * session. If the timestamp is after the session close, it is grouped with the next day's session.\n *\n * <p>Example usage:\n *\n * <pre>{@code\n * DataStream<TradeEvent> trades = ...;\n * KeyedStream<TradeEvent, String> keyed = trades.keyBy(TradeEvent::getSymbol);\n * WindowedStream<TradeEvent, String, TimeWindow> windowed =\n *   keyed.window(PricingSessionWindow.forMarket(\n *       \"NYSE\",\n *       ZoneId.of(\"America/New_York\"),\n *       LocalTime.of(9, 30),\n *       LocalTime.of(16, 0)));\n * }</pre>\n */\n@PublicEvolving\npublic class PricingSessionWindow extends MergingWindowAssigner<Object, TimeWindow> {\n\n    private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;\n\n    private final String marketId;\n    private final ZoneId timezone;\n    private final LocalTime sessionOpen;\n    private final LocalTime sessionClose;\n\n    protected PricingSessionWindow(\n            String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime sessionOpen, LocalTime sessionClose) {\n        if (marketId == null || marketId.isEmpty()) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"marketId must not be null or empty\");\n        }\n        if (timezone == null) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"timezone must not be null\");\n        }\n        if (sessionOpen == null || sessionClose == null) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"sessionOpen and sessionClose must not be null\");\n        }\n        if (!sessionOpen.isBefore(sessionClose)) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\n                    \"sessionOpen must be before sessionClose; for overnight sessions \"\n                            + \"spanning midnight, split into two windows\");\n        }\n        this.marketId = marketId;\n        this.timezone = timezone;\n        this.sessionOpen = sessionOpen;\n        this.sessionClose = sessionClose;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a new {@code PricingSessionWindow} for the given market.\n     *\n     * @param marketId A human-readable market identifier (e.g., \"NYSE\", \"LSE\").\n     * @param timezone The timezone in which the session hours are expressed.\n     * @param open The local time at which the session opens (inclusive).\n     * @param close The local time at which the session closes (exclusive).\n     * @return The configured {@code PricingSessionWindow} assigner.\n     */\n    public static PricingSessionWindow forMarket(\n            String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime open, LocalTime close) {\n        return new PricingSessionWindow(marketId, timezone, open, close);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Collection<TimeWindow> assignWindows(\n            Object element, long timestamp, WindowAssignerContext context) {\n        // Convert epoch milliseconds to a ZonedDateTime in the market's timezone\n        ZonedDateTime eventTime =\n                Instant.ofEpochMilli(timestamp).atZone(timezone);\n\n        LocalDate eventDate = eventTime.toLocalDate();\n        LocalTime eventLocalTime = eventTime.toLocalTime();\n\n        LocalDate sessionDate;\n        if (eventLocalTime.compareTo(sessionClose) >= 0) {\n            // After session close: assign to next trading day's session\n            sessionDate = eventDate.plusDays(1);\n        } else {\n            // Before or during session: assign to current day's session\n            sessionDate = eventDate;\n        }\n\n        ZonedDateTime windowStart = ZonedDateTime.of(\n                LocalDateTime.of(sessionDate, sessionOpen), timezone);\n        ZonedDateTime windowEnd = ZonedDateTime.of(\n                LocalDateTime.of(sessionDate, sessionClose), timezone);\n\n        long startMs = windowStart.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n        long endMs = windowEnd.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n\n        return Collections.singletonList(new TimeWindow(startMs, endMs));\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Trigger<Object, TimeWindow> getDefaultTrigger() {\n        return EventTimeTrigger.create();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public TypeSerializer<TimeWindow> getWindowSerializer(ExecutionConfig executionConfig) {\n        return new TimeWindow.Serializer();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isEventTime() {\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    /** Merge overlapping {@link TimeWindow}s. */\n    @Override\n    public void mergeWindows(\n            Collection<TimeWindow> windows, MergingWindowAssigner.MergeCallback<TimeWindow> c) {\n        TimeWindow.mergeWindows(windows, c);\n    }\n\n    public String getMarketId() {\n        return marketId;\n    }\n\n    public ZoneId getTimezone() {\n        return timezone;\n    }\n\n    public LocalTime getSessionOpen() {\n        return sessionOpen;\n    }\n\n    public LocalTime getSessionClose() {\n        return sessionClose;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return \"PricingSessionWindow(\"\n                + \"marketId='\" + marketId + \"'\"\n                + \", timezone=\" + timezone\n                + \", open=\" + sessionOpen\n                + \", close=\" + sessionClose\n                + \")\";\n    }\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":3,"cache_creation_input_tokens":374,"cache_read_input_tokens":51341,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":374,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"ad959432-8d0f-4bcd-be8e-1a104e7900c9","uuid":"db2fa8fd-19a8-4157-b9d4-5e6bbecc38d3"}

org.apache.flink.api.common.state.ValueState;\nimport org.apache.flink.api.common.state.ValueStateDescriptor;\nimport org.apache.flink.api.common.typeinfo.Types;\nimport org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.windows.TimeWindow;\n\n/**\n * A {@link Trigger} for use with {@link\n * org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.assigners.PricingSessionWindow} that fires at market\n * close (the end of the session window) using event-time timers.\n *\n * <p>This trigger also supports early firing on configurable events such as circuit breaker halts,\n * enabling downstream operators to react to extraordinary market conditions before the session ends.\n *\n * <p>The trigger supports merging ({@link #canMerge()} returns {@code true}) and correctly\n * re-registers timers on window merges via {@link #onMerge(TimeWindow, OnMergeContext)}.\n */\n@PublicEvolving\npublic class PricingSessionTrigger extends Trigger<Object, TimeWindow> {\n\n    private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;\n\n    /**\n     * State descriptor used to track whether an early-fire has been requested for this window\n     * (e.g., due to a circuit breaker halt signal).\n     */\n    private static final ValueStateDescriptor<Boolean> EARLY_FIRE_STATE =\n            new ValueStateDescriptor<>(\"pricing-session-early-fire\", Types.BOOLEAN);\n\n    private PricingSessionTrigger() {}\n\n    @Override\n    public TriggerResult onElement(\n            Object element, long timestamp, TimeWindow window, TriggerContext ctx)\n            throws Exception {\n        // Check if an early fire has been requested for this window\n        ValueState<Boolean> earlyFireState = ctx.getPartitionedState(EARLY_FIRE_STATE);\n        Boolean earlyFire = earlyFireState.value();\n        if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(earlyFire)) {\n            // Clear the early-fire flag and fire immediately\n            earlyFireState.clear();\n            return TriggerResult.FIRE;\n        }\n\n        if (window.maxTimestamp() <= ctx.getCurrentWatermark()) {\n            // Watermark already past the window end: fire immediately\n            return TriggerResult.FIRE;\n        } else {\n            // Register a timer for the market close (window end)\n            ctx.registerEventTimeTimer(window.maxTimestamp());\n            return TriggerResult.CONTINUE;\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public TriggerResult onEventTime(long time, TimeWindow window, TriggerContext ctx)\n            throws Exception {\n        // Fire when the watermark passes the session close time\n        return time == window.maxTimestamp() ? TriggerResult.FIRE : TriggerResult.CONTINUE;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public TriggerResult onProcessingTime(long time, TimeWindow window, TriggerContext ctx)\n            throws Exception {\n        return TriggerResult.CONTINUE;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean canMerge() {\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onMerge(TimeWindow window, OnMergeContext ctx) throws Exception {\n        // Merge the early-fire state from constituent windows into the merged window\n        ctx.mergePartitionedState(EARLY_FIRE_STATE);\n\n        // Re-register the timer for the merged window's end (market close)\n        long windowMaxTimestamp = window.maxTimestamp();\n        if (windowMaxTimestamp > ctx.getCurrentWatermark()) {\n            ctx.registerEventTimeTimer(windowMaxTimestamp);\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void clear(TimeWindow window, TriggerContext ctx) throws Exception {\n        // Delete the event-time timer and clean up state\n        ctx.deleteEventTimeTimer(window.maxTimestamp());\n        ctx.getPartitionedState(EARLY_FIRE_STATE).clear();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Signals that an early fire should occur for the window containing the next element. This can\n     * be called externally when a circuit breaker halt or other extraordinary event is detected.\n     *\n     * @param ctx The trigger context for the current window.\n     * @throws Exception if state access fails.\n     */\n    public void signalEarlyFire(TriggerContext ctx) throws Exception {\n        ctx.getPartitionedState(EARLY_FIRE_STATE).update(Boolean.TRUE);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return \"PricingSessionTrigger()\";\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a new {@code PricingSessionTrigger} that fires at market close (the end of the\n     * session window).\n     */\n    public static PricingSessionTrigger create() {\n        return new PricingSessionTrigger();\n    }\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":3,"cache_creation_input_tokens":374,"cache_read_input_tokens":51341,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":374,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"ad959432-8d0f-4bcd-be8e-1a104e7900c9","uuid":"424ceba5-4832-4a08-accd-f174ff9a6db8"}

You may obtain a copy of the License at\n *\n * http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0\n *\n * Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software\n * distributed under the License is distributed on an \"AS IS\" BASIS,\n * WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.\n * See the License for the specific language governing permissions and\n * limitations under the License.\n */\n\npackage org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.assigners;\n\nimport org.apache.flink.annotation.PublicEvolving;\nimport org.apache.flink.api.common.ExecutionConfig;\nimport org.apache.flink.api.common.typeutils.TypeSerializer;\nimport org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.triggers.EventTimeTrigger;\nimport org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.triggers.Trigger;\nimport org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.windows.TimeWindow;\n\nimport java.time.Instant;\nimport java.time.LocalDate;\nimport java.time.LocalDateTime;\nimport java.time.LocalTime;\nimport java.time.ZoneId;\nimport java.time.ZonedDateTime;\nimport java.util.Collection;\nimport java.util.Collections;\n\n/**\n * A {@link WindowAssigner} that windows trading events into fixed market session windows based on\n * the timestamp of the elements. Each window corresponds to a single trading day's session\n * (e.g., NYSE 09:30-16:00 ET, LSE 08:00-16:30 GMT).\n *\n * <p>Events are assigned to the session window for the trading day that their timestamp falls in.\n * If an event's timestamp is before the session open on a given day, it is grouped with that day's\n * session. If the timestamp is after the session close, it is grouped with the next day's session.\n *\n * <p>Example usage:\n *\n * <pre>{@code\n * DataStream<TradeEvent> trades = ...;\n * KeyedStream<TradeEvent, String> keyed = trades.keyBy(TradeEvent::getSymbol);\n * WindowedStream<TradeEvent, String, TimeWindow> windowed =\n *   keyed.window(PricingSessionWindow.forMarket(\n *       \"NYSE\",\n *       ZoneId.of(\"America/New_York\"),\n *       LocalTime.of(9, 30),\n *       LocalTime.of(16, 0)));\n * }</pre>\n */\n@PublicEvolving\npublic class PricingSessionWindow extends MergingWindowAssigner<Object, TimeWindow> {\n\n    private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;\n\n    private final String marketId;\n    private final ZoneId timezone;\n    private final LocalTime sessionOpen;\n    private final LocalTime sessionClose;\n\n    protected PricingSessionWindow(\n            String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime sessionOpen, LocalTime sessionClose) {\n        if (marketId == null || marketId.isEmpty()) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"marketId must not be null or empty\");\n        }\n        if (timezone == null) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"timezone must not be null\");\n        }\n        if (sessionOpen == null || sessionClose == null) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"sessionOpen and sessionClose must not be null\");\n        }\n        if (!sessionOpen.isBefore(sessionClose)) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\n                    \"sessionOpen must be before sessionClose; for overnight sessions \"\n                            + \"spanning midnight, split into two windows\");\n        }\n        this.marketId = marketId;\n        this.timezone = timezone;\n        this.sessionOpen = sessionOpen;\n        this.sessionClose = sessionClose;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a new {@code PricingSessionWindow} for the given market.\n     *\n     * @param marketId A human-readable market identifier (e.g., \"NYSE\", \"LSE\").\n     * @param timezone The timezone in which the session hours are expressed.\n     * @param open The local time at which the session opens (inclusive).\n     * @param close The local time at which the session closes (exclusive).\n     * @return The configured {@code PricingSessionWindow} assigner.\n     */\n    public static PricingSessionWindow forMarket(\n            String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime open, LocalTime close) {\n        return new PricingSessionWindow(marketId, timezone, open, close);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Collection<TimeWindow> assignWindows(\n            Object element, long timestamp, WindowAssignerContext context) {\n        // Convert epoch milliseconds to a ZonedDateTime in the market's timezone\n        ZonedDateTime eventTime =\n                Instant.ofEpochMilli(timestamp).atZone(timezone);\n\n        LocalDate eventDate = eventTime.toLocalDate();\n        LocalTime eventLocalTime = eventTime.toLocalTime();\n\n        LocalDate sessionDate;\n        if (eventLocalTime.compareTo(sessionClose) >= 0) {\n            // After session close: assign to next trading day's session\n            sessionDate = eventDate.plusDays(1);\n        } else {\n            // Before or during session: assign to current day's session\n            sessionDate = eventDate;\n        }\n\n        ZonedDateTime windowStart = ZonedDateTime.of(\n                LocalDateTime.of(sessionDate, sessionOpen), timezone);\n        ZonedDateTime windowEnd = ZonedDateTime.of(\n                LocalDateTime.of(sessionDate, sessionClose), timezone);\n\n        long startMs = windowStart.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n        long endMs = windowEnd.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n\n        return Collections.singletonList(new TimeWindow(startMs, endMs));\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Trigger<Object, TimeWindow> getDefaultTrigger() {\n        return EventTimeTrigger.create();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public TypeSerializer<TimeWindow> getWindowSerializer(ExecutionConfig executionConfig) {\n        return new TimeWindow.Serializer();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isEventTime() {\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    /** Merge overlapping {@link TimeWindow}s. */\n    @Override\n    public void mergeWindows(\n            Collection<TimeWindow> windows, MergingWindowAssigner.MergeCallback<TimeWindow> c) {\n        TimeWindow.mergeWindows(windows, c);\n    }\n\n    public String getMarketId() {\n        return marketId;\n    }\n\n    public ZoneId getTimezone() {\n        return timezone;\n    }\n\n    public LocalTime getSessionOpen() {\n        return sessionOpen;\n    }\n\n    public LocalTime getSessionClose() {\n        return sessionClose;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return \"PricingSessionWindow(\"\n                + \"marketId='\" + marketId + \"'\"\n                + \", timezone=\" + timezone\n                + \", open=\" + sessionOpen\n                + \", close=\" + sessionClose\n                + \")\";\n    }\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

org.apache.flink.api.common.state.ValueState;\nimport org.apache.flink.api.common.state.ValueStateDescriptor;\nimport org.apache.flink.api.common.typeinfo.Types;\nimport org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.windows.TimeWindow;\n\n/**\n * A {@link Trigger} for use with {@link\n * org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.assigners.PricingSessionWindow} that fires at market\n * close (the end of the session window) using event-time timers.\n *\n * <p>This trigger also supports early firing on configurable events such as circuit breaker halts,\n * enabling downstream operators to react to extraordinary market conditions before the session ends.\n *\n * <p>The trigger supports merging ({@link #canMerge()} returns {@code true}) and correctly\n * re-registers timers on window merges via {@link #onMerge(TimeWindow, OnMergeContext)}.\n */\n@PublicEvolving\npublic class PricingSessionTrigger extends Trigger<Object, TimeWindow> {\n\n    private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;\n\n    /**\n     * State descriptor used to track whether an early-fire has been requested for this window\n     * (e.g., due to a circuit breaker halt signal).\n     */\n    private static final ValueStateDescriptor<Boolean> EARLY_FIRE_STATE =\n            new ValueStateDescriptor<>(\"pricing-session-early-fire\", Types.BOOLEAN);\n\n    private PricingSessionTrigger() {}\n\n    @Override\n    public TriggerResult onElement(\n            Object element, long timestamp, TimeWindow window, TriggerContext ctx)\n            throws Exception {\n        // Check if an early fire has been requested for this window\n        ValueState<Boolean> earlyFireState = ctx.getPartitionedState(EARLY_FIRE_STATE);\n        Boolean earlyFire = earlyFireState.value();\n        if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(earlyFire)) {\n            // Clear the early-fire flag and fire immediately\n            earlyFireState.clear();\n            return TriggerResult.FIRE;\n        }\n\n        if (window.maxTimestamp() <= ctx.getCurrentWatermark()) {\n            // Watermark already past the window end: fire immediately\n            return TriggerResult.FIRE;\n        } else {\n            // Register a timer for the market close (window end)\n            ctx.registerEventTimeTimer(window.maxTimestamp());\n            return TriggerResult.CONTINUE;\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public TriggerResult onEventTime(long time, TimeWindow window, TriggerContext ctx)\n            throws Exception {\n        // Fire when the watermark passes the session close time\n        return time == window.maxTimestamp() ? TriggerResult.FIRE : TriggerResult.CONTINUE;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public TriggerResult onProcessingTime(long time, TimeWindow window, TriggerContext ctx)\n            throws Exception {\n        return TriggerResult.CONTINUE;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean canMerge() {\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onMerge(TimeWindow window, OnMergeContext ctx) throws Exception {\n        // Merge the early-fire state from constituent windows into the merged window\n        ctx.mergePartitionedState(EARLY_FIRE_STATE);\n\n        // Re-register the timer for the merged window's end (market close)\n        long windowMaxTimestamp = window.maxTimestamp();\n        if (windowMaxTimestamp > ctx.getCurrentWatermark()) {\n            ctx.registerEventTimeTimer(windowMaxTimestamp);\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void clear(TimeWindow window, TriggerContext ctx) throws Exception {\n        // Delete the event-time timer and clean up state\n        ctx.deleteEventTimeTimer(window.maxTimestamp());\n        ctx.getPartitionedState(EARLY_FIRE_STATE).clear();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Signals that an early fire should occur for the window containing the next element. This can\n     * be called externally when a circuit breaker halt or other extraordinary event is detected.\n     *\n     * @param ctx The trigger context for the current window.\n     * @throws Exception if state access fails.\n     */\n    public void signalEarlyFire(TriggerContext ctx) throws Exception {\n        ctx.getPartitionedState(EARLY_FIRE_STATE).update(Boolean.TRUE);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return \"PricingSessionTrigger()\";\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a new {@code PricingSessionTrigger} that fires at market close (the end of the\n     * session window).\n     */\n    public static PricingSessionTrigger create() {\n        return new PricingSessionTrigger();\n    }\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

event-time timestamp into a fixed `TimeWindow` representing a single trading session:\n\n1. **Timezone conversion**: Uses Java's `ZonedDateTime` + `ZoneId` to convert epoch milliseconds to a local time in the market's timezone, correctly handling DST transitions.\n\n2. **Session date determination**:\n   - If the event timestamp falls **before or during** the session (local time < sessionClose), it is assigned to the **current day's** session window.\n   - If the event timestamp falls **after** the session close (local time >= sessionClose), it is assigned to the **next day's** session window. This handles post-market events correctly.\n\n3. **Window boundaries**: The resulting `TimeWindow(sessionOpenMs, sessionCloseMs)` uses epoch milliseconds for the session open and close on the determined trading day.\n\n4. **Merging**: Since all events within the same trading day produce identical `TimeWindow` instances (same start/end), `TimeWindow.mergeWindows()` handles the standard overlapping/consecutive window consolidation as used by session windows.\n\n### PricingSessionTrigger Design\n\nModeled directly after `EventTimeTrigger` with additions for capital markets:\n\n- **Normal firing**: Fires when the watermark passes `window.maxTimestamp()` (market close time), via `ctx.registerEventTimeTimer(window.maxTimestamp())`.\n- **Early firing**: Supports circuit breaker halts or other extraordinary events via `signalEarlyFire(ctx)` which sets a `ValueState<Boolean>` flag. On the next `onElement()` call, the trigger detects the flag and fires immediately.\n- **Merge support**: `canMerge()` returns `true`; `onMerge()` merges the early-fire state partition and re-registers the timer for the merged window's end timestamp.\n- **Cleanup**: `clear()` deletes the event-time timer and clears the early-fire state.\n\n### TradingSessionExtractor Design\n\nA `@FunctionalInterface` extending `Serializable`, modeled after `SessionWindowTimeGapExtractor`. It enables dynamic routing of stream elements to different markets without requiring separate keyed streams per market — the extractor can be composed with a dynamic `PricingSessionWindow` variant to support multi-market topologies.\n\n### Integration with Flink Windowing Architecture\n\nAll three classes integrate cleanly with Flink's existing windowing framework:\n- `PricingSessionWindow` extends `MergingWindowAssigner<Object, TimeWindow>` from `flink-runtime`, consistent with `EventTimeSessionWindows`\n- `PricingSessionTrigger` extends `Trigger<Object, TimeWindow>` from `flink-runtime`, consistent with `EventTimeTrigger`\n- Both classes are placed in `flink-streaming-java` (higher-level module), not `flink-runtime` (lower-level), matching the placement of `EventTimeSessionWindows` and other concrete window implementations\n- Imports only use classes already present in the Flink dependency graph (`java.time.*`, `flink-runtime` windowing classes)\nSOLUTION_EOF\necho \"Solution written to /logs/agent/solution.md\"","description":"Write solution.md to /logs/agent/"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":343,"cache_read_input_tokens":55983,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":343,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":24,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"ad959432-8d0f-4bcd-be8e-1a104e7900c9","uuid":"4c89f550-74ab-4fea-a960-71e56129caf8"}
